# Obtaining prop test vectors for Nu5

We need hex representation of a block that haves V5 transactions with orchard data.
We are also looking to get a block with V4 and V5 transaction and with sapling data, resuming: the most complete as possible.

Currently we have a test block round trip that we can use for this purpose at https://github.com/ZcashFoundation/zebra/blob/v1.0.0-alpha.8/zebra-chain/src/block/tests/prop.rs#L81

Here we made this temporal modifications to get the data we need at the top of the test:

```rust
..
// print the block structure
dbg!(&block);

let bytes = block.zcash_serialize_to_vec()?;
use core::fmt::Write;
let mut s = String::with_capacity(2 * bytes.len());
for byte in bytes {
  write!(s, "{:02X}", byte)?;
}
// print the hex string
dbg!(s);
```

## Test vectors

### GENERATED_V5_1
